      && tar -xzf apache-ant-1.10.12-bin.tar.gz \
      && mv apache-ant-1.10.12 /opt/ant \
      && rm apache-ant-1.10.12-bin.tar.gz
  ENV PATH="/opt/ant/bin:${PATH}"
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash devuser
  USER devuser
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/SymMC
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

      build-essential \
      wget \
      ca-certificates \
      libz-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN mkdir -p /tmp/minisat \
      && cd /tmp/minisat \
      && wget https://github.com/msoos/minisat/archive/refs/tags/releases/2.2.0.tar.gz -O minisat.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf minisat.tar.gz --strip-components=1 \
      && mkdir -p build \
      && cd build \
      && cmake .. \
      && make \
      && make install \
      && cd / \
      && rm -rf /tmp/minisat
  RUN wget https://archive.apache.org/dist/ant/binaries/apache-ant-1.10.12-bin.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf apache-ant-1.10.12-bin.tar.gz \
      && mv apache-ant-1.10.12 /opt/ant \
      && rm apache-ant-1.10.12-bin.tar.gz
  ENV PATH="/opt/ant/bin:${PATH}"
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash devuser
  USER devuser
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/SymMC
  COPY --chown=devuser:devuser . .
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS builder
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/SymMC
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      openjdk-8-jdk \
      cmake \
      git \
      gcc \
      g++ \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      build-essential \
      wget \
      ca-certificates \
      libz-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN mkdir -p /tmp/minisat \
      && cd /tmp/minisat \
      && wget https://github.com/msoos/minisat/archive/refs/tags/releases/2.2.0.tar.gz -O minisat.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf minisat.tar.gz --strip-components=1 \
      && ls -la \
      && if [ ! -f CMakeLists.txt ]; then \
          echo "Downloading CMakeLists.txt" \
          && wget https://raw.githubusercontent.com/msoos/minisat/master/CMakeLists.txt; \
         fi \
      && mkdir build \
      && cd build \
      && cmake .. \
      && make \
      && make install \
      && cd / \
      && rm -rf /tmp/minisat
  RUN wget https://archive.apache.org/dist/ant/binaries/apache-ant-1.10.12-bin.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf apache-ant-1.10.12-bin.tar.gz \
      && mv apache-ant-1.10.12 /opt/ant \
      && rm apache-ant-1.10.12-bin.tar.gz
  ENV PATH="/opt/ant/bin:${PATH}"
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash devuser
  USER devuser
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/SymMC
  COPY --chown=devuser:devuser . .
  RUN cd Enhanced_Kodkod \
      && chmod +x build.sh \
      && ./build.sh
  RUN cd Enumerator_Estimator \
      && chmod +x build.sh \
      && ./build.sh
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS builder
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/SymMC
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      openjdk-8-jdk \
      cmake \
      git \
      gcc \
      g++ \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      build-essential \
      wget \
      ca-certificates \
      libz-dev \
      libgmp-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN mkdir -p /tmp/minisat \
      && cd /tmp/minisat \
      && wget https://github.com/msoos/minisat/archive/refs/tags/releases/2.2.0.tar.gz -O minisat.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf minisat.tar.gz --strip-components=1 \
      && mkdir build \
      && cd build \
      && cmake -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release .. \
      && make -j$(nproc) \
      && make install \
      && ldconfig \
      && cd / \
      && rm -rf /tmp/minisat
  RUN wget https://archive.apache.org/dist/ant/binaries/apache-ant-1.10.12-bin.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf apache-ant-1.10.12-bin.tar.gz \
      && mv apache-ant-1.10.12 /opt/ant \
      && rm apache-ant-1.10.12-bin.tar.gz
  ENV PATH="/opt/ant/bin:${PATH}"
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/usr/lib/jvm/java-8-openjdk-amd64
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash devuser
  USER devuser
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/SymMC
  COPY --chown=devuser:devuser . .
  RUN cd Enhanced_Kodkod \
      && chmod +x build.sh \
      && ./build.sh
  RUN cd Enumerator_Estimator \
      && chmod +x build.sh \
      && ./build.sh
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

      && wget https://github.com/msoos/minisat/archive/refs/tags/releases/2.2.0.tar.gz -O minisat.tar.gz \

      && mkdir -p build \
      && cd build \
      && cmake .. \
      && make -j$(nproc) \
      && make install \
      && ldconfig \
      && cd / \

      && tar -xzf apache-ant-1.10.12-bin.tar.gz \
      && mv apache-ant-1.10.12 /opt/ant \

  USER devuser
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/SymMC
  COPY --chown=devuser:devuser . .
  RUN cd Enhanced_Kodkod \
      && chmod +x build.sh \
      && ./build.sh \
      && cd ../Enumerator_Estimator \
      && chmod +x build.sh \
      && bash -x ./build.sh
  USER root
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/SymMC
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS builder
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/SymMC

      openjdk-8-jdk \
      cmake \
      git \
      gcc \
      g++ \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      build-essential \

      ca-certificates \

      unzip \

      && unzip minisat.zip -d /tmp/minisat \
      && cd /tmp/minisat/minisat-releases-2.2.0 \
      && mkdir -p build \
      && cd build \
      && cmake -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release -DCMAKE_INSTALL_PREFIX=/usr/local . \
      && make -j$(nproc) \
      && make install \
      && ldconfig \
      && cd / \
      && rm -rf /tmp/minisat*
  RUN wget https://archive.apache.org/dist/ant/binaries/apache-ant-1.10.12-bin.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf apache-ant-1.10.12-bin.tar.gz \
      && mv apache-ant-1.10.12 /opt/ant \
      && rm apache-ant-1.10.12-bin.tar.gz
  ENV PATH="/opt/ant/bin:${PATH}"
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/usr/lib/jvm/java-8-openjdk-amd64
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash devuser
  USER devuser
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/SymMC
  COPY --chown=devuser:devuser . .
  RUN cd Enhanced_Kodkod \
      && chmod +x build.sh \
      && bash -x ./build.sh || true \
      && cd ../Enumerator_Estimator \
      && chmod +x build.sh \
      && bash -x ./build.sh || true
  USER root
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/SymMC
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

      && sed -i 's/friend Lit mkLit(Var var, bool sign = false);/friend Lit mkLit(Var var, bool sign);/' core/SolverTypes.h \

      && echo "project(minisat)" >> CMakeLists.txt \
      && echo "set(CMAKE_CXX_FLAGS \"\${CMAKE_CXX_FLAGS} -Wno-literal-suffix\")" >> CMakeLists.txt \

      && echo "    core/Solver.cc" >> CMakeLists.txt \
      && echo "    core/SolverTypes.h" >> CMakeLists.txt \

      && echo "install(TARGETS minisat DESTINATION lib)" >> CMakeLists.txt \

      && mkdir -p build \
      && cd build \
